---
owner: Codex 总控
status: draft
purpose: Define which files are the formal truth by layer and which files are only implementation projections.
layer: L0 SSOT
---

# Source Of Truth Map

## Global Rule
- Formal truth lives in `docs/`.
- Implementation lives in `apps/`.
- Derived projections may live in `packages/`.
- Temporary analysis and extracted input copies must live outside formal truth, under ignored temp space only.

## Current Round Registrations

### Coverage Rule For The Current Control Package

- The `三板块主线签收 + enterprise_hub V1 successor re-entry` control package now formally covers:
  - `docs/00_ssot/three_board_real_chain_result_verification_dispatch_round1.md` as the dispatch basis
  - `docs/00_ssot/three_board_real_chain_verification_checklist_v1.md` as the canonical verification template
  - `docs/00_ssot/three_board_real_chain_result_verification_rerun_addendum.md` as the current rerun result receipt
  - `docs/00_ssot/three_board_mainline_integration_release_review_conclusion_addendum.md` as the current control-signoff conclusion
  - `docs/00_ssot/three_board_mainline_maintenance_only_follow_up_judgment_addendum.md` as the post-signoff maintenance-only ruling
  - `docs/00_ssot/post_three_board_next_active_board_ruling_addendum.md` as the next-active-board selection ruling
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_reentry_stage_gate_checklist_addendum.md` as the successor-board gate checklist
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_bounded_reentry_dispatch_bundle_addendum.md` as the successor-board bounded dispatch basis
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_backend_residual_risk_closure_execution_prompt_addendum.md` as the backend role prompt for successor-board residual-risk closure
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_bff_residual_risk_closure_execution_prompt_addendum.md` as the BFF role prompt for successor-board residual-risk closure
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_frontend_residual_risk_closure_execution_prompt_addendum.md` as the frontend role prompt for successor-board residual-risk closure
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_frontend_residual_risk_closure_receipt_addendum.md` as the current local frontend execution receipt for successor-board residual-risk closure
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_residual_risk_closure_result_verification_dispatch_addendum.md` as the current independent verification dispatch basis for successor-board residual-risk closure
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_integration_risk_closure_review_conclusion_addendum.md` as the current control-signoff conclusion for successor-board residual-risk closure
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_post_risk_closure_stage_gate_checklist_addendum.md` as the current stage gate checklist after successor-board residual-risk closure
  - `docs/00_ssot/enterprise_hub_v1_post_risk_closure_bounded_next_stage_dispatch_bundle_addendum.md` as the current bounded next-stage dispatch bundle after successor-board residual-risk closure
- These files are the prerequisite ruling set for:
  - judging whether `项目发布工作台 / 项目发布 / 项目展示` have real development-stage runtime evidence on the frozen tunnel entry
  - separating canonical API hits from page-layer demo fallback
  - deciding whether the current verified scope may proceed to `联调发布` as a development-stage step
  - freezing the exact passed scope, retained vetoes, current successor board, the three role-specific execution prompts, the current receipt intake, the independent verification dispatch, the current review conclusion, the post-risk-closure gate, and the current bounded next-stage dispatch now governing `enterprise_hub V1`
- These files do not by themselves approve:
  - production release
  - launch readiness
  - scope expansion beyond the current verified three-board mainline
  - enterprise_hub residual-risk closure completion before role receipts and independent verification are re-run
  - enterprise_hub `release-prep` until a new stage gate explicitly says so
  - direct implementation of the `项目展示筛选与创建表单重构` object
  - direct implementation of the `订单承接与履约承接主链` object

  - direct implementation
  - release-prep
  - production release

### Coverage Rule For The Package

- The `已认证主体资料更正 / 重认证能力` package now formally covers:
  - `docs/01_contracts/**` for the canonical `certification/revalidate` write contract and related readback clarification
  - `docs/02_backend/**` for `Server` truth ownership, audit carrier, and current-formal-truth update rules
  - `docs/03_bff/**` for app-facing forwarding and controlled error normalization only
  - `docs/04_frontend/**` for the approved-state entry, Chinese copy, and formal-vs-preview UI split
  - `apps/server/**`, `apps/bff/**`, and `apps/mobile/**` as downstream implementation consumers only
- These files are the prerequisite ruling set for:
  - giving approved organizations a formal certification-correction path
  - keeping `项目工作台 / 项目发布 / 项目展示` tied to current effective certification truth during correction attempts
  - recording correction attempts without introducing a second certification truth root
- These files do not approve:
  - delayed review queues
  - pending shadow certification truth
  - BFF-owned or Flutter-owned qualification state
  - payment, deposit, billing, or settlement work

### 2026-04-10 Project Transaction Skeleton P0 Package

- [project_transaction_skeleton_p0_gate_checklist.md](/Users/wangweiwei/Desktop/展览装修之家总控/docs/00_ssot/project_transaction_skeleton_p0_gate_checklist.md) is the formal `L0` stage gate for `项目交易骨架 P0`, freezing passed gates, failed gates, veto gates, the active-runtime evidence baseline, and the only allowed next-stage entry.
- [project_transaction_skeleton_p0_implementation_unlock_addendum.md](/Users/wangweiwei/Desktop/展览装修之家总控/docs/00_ssot/project_transaction_skeleton_p0_implementation_unlock_addendum.md) is the formal `L0` implementation unlock ruling for `项目交易骨架 P0`, freezing either allowed or blocked status and the exact bounded implementation scope.
- [project_transaction_skeleton_p0_contracts_addendum.md](/Users/wangweiwei/Desktop/展览装修之家总控/docs/01_contracts/project_transaction_skeleton_p0_contracts_addendum.md) is the formal `L2` contracts freeze for the `P0` trade skeleton path family, object boundary, read-vs-write split, and explicit non-P0 prohibition list.
- [project_transaction_skeleton_p0_backend_truth_addendum.md](/Users/wangweiwei/Desktop/展览装修之家总控/docs/02_backend/project_transaction_skeleton_p0_backend_truth_addendum.md) is the formal `L3 Backend` truth freeze for `P0`, freezing truth ownership, persistence carriers, canonical-vs-derived split, audit ownership, and prohibited truth mixing.
- [project_transaction_skeleton_p0_bff_surface_addendum.md](/Users/wangweiwei/Desktop/展览装修之家总控/docs/03_bff/project_transaction_skeleton_p0_bff_surface_addendum.md) is the formal `L4 BFF` surface freeze for `P0`, freezing app-facing shaping, auth shaping, error normalization, and the hard rule that `BFF` must not own a second trade-state machine.
- [project_transaction_skeleton_p0_frontend_surface_addendum.md](/Users/wangweiwei/Desktop/展览装修之家总控/docs/04_frontend/project_transaction_skeleton_p0_frontend_surface_addendum.md) is the formal `L5 Frontend` surface freeze for `P0`, freezing Flutter page/route admission, UI-guard vs final-truth split, handoff graph, and prohibited copy.

### Coverage Rule For The Package

- The `项目交易骨架 P0` package now formally covers:
  - `docs/01_contracts/**` for the P0 trade-skeleton path family and object boundary
  - `docs/02_backend/**` for the P0 truth-owner and persistence-carrier boundary
  - `docs/03_bff/**` for the P0 app-facing shaping boundary
  - `docs/04_frontend/**` for the Flutter-side P0 page and interaction boundary
  - `apps/server/**`, `apps/bff/**`, and `apps/mobile/**` as downstream implementation consumers only
- These files are the prerequisite ruling set for:
  - any future `项目交易骨架 P0` bounded implementation
  - any later `payment / billing / deposit / guarantee / credit` admission judgment
- These files do not by themselves approve:
  - `payment / billing / settlement`
  - `project visibility/displayStatus runtime`
  - `project review state machine runtime`

### 2026-04-10 Debug Whitelist Session Package

- [debug_whitelist_session_unlock_addendum.md](/Users/wangweiwei/Desktop/展览装修之家总控/docs/00_ssot/debug_whitelist_session_unlock_addendum.md) is the formal `L0` boundary freeze for `联调白名单测试会话`, freezing that it is a temporary integration-testing capability rather than a formal user feature, and that it may bypass OTP only but never bypass `Server`-owned session truth.

### Coverage Rule For The Package

- The `联调白名单测试会话` package now formally covers:
  - `docs/01_contracts/**` for the controlled app-facing debug session contract
  - `docs/02_backend/**` for session-truth ownership and audit/revoke/expire rules
  - `docs/03_bff/**` for forwarding and shaping boundary only
- These files do not approve:
  - Flutter-local fake session
  - `BFF`-owned session truth
  - production default bypass

## Non-truth Inputs
- `.tmp/input_extracts/**` is reserved for extracted source material and analysis copies.
- Files in `.tmp/input_extracts/**` are explicitly non-SSOT and must never be cited as the final project truth.

## Cross-layer Change Order
1. Update `docs/00_ssot` if naming, scope, hierarchy, or constitutions change.
2. Update `docs/01_contracts` if external interfaces or config truth change.
3. Update `docs/02_backend`, `docs/03_bff`, `docs/04_frontend`, and `docs/05_admin` as needed.
4. Update implementation in `apps/**`.
5. Update generated projections in `packages/**` only after upstream truth is frozen.

## Gate Execution Rule
- `docs/00_ssot/gate_register_v1.md` is the formal gate register.
- Codex 总控 must submit a stage gate checklist before any new stage prompt bundle.
- Cloud workspaces mirror truth and may not become a second authoring root.
